  <script>
   // =================================================================
		// Combined section starts

		// Combined timeout
		var HB_TIMEOUT = 2000;

		var PREBID_TIMEOUT = HB_TIMEOUT;
		var CDB_TIMEOUT = HB_TIMEOUT;


		window.hb_status = {
		    n_adserver_callback: [],
		    adserverRequestSent: false,
            prebidTargetingSet: false
		};
		  
		function adServerCallback(source) {
		    if (window.hb_status.adserverRequestSent) return;
		    // add source to the processed list
		    window.hb_status.n_adserver_callback.push(source);
		    if (source == 'prebid') {
		        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
		            pbjs.que.push(function() {
		                pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
                        	window.hb_status.prebidTargetingSet = true;
		            });
		        });
		    } else if (source == 'criteo') {
		        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
		            Criteo.SetDFPKeyValueTargeting();
		        });
		    }
		  console.log('called by ' + source);
		  
		    if (window.hb_status.n_adserver_callback.length >= 2
		            || "timeout" == source) {
		            //move out from cmd.push to fix FF refresh bug
		            window.hb_status.adserverRequestSent = true;
		        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                    if (!window.hb_status.prebidTargetingSet) {
                        pbjs.que.push(function() {
                            pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync(); 
                        });
                    }
		            //googletag.pubads().refresh();
		            refreshByAdUnit();
		            console.log('googletag refreshed by ' + source);
		        });
		    };
		  
		}

		function refreshByAdUnit(){
			if(typeof googleAd_OSV != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_OSV]);
			if(typeof googleAd_MR1 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_MR1]);
			if(typeof googleAd_MR2 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_MR2]);
			if(typeof googleAd_MR3 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_MR3]);								
			if(typeof googleAd_MR4 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_MR4]);
			if(typeof googleAd_LB1 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_LB1]);
			if(typeof googleAd_LB2 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_LB2]);
			if(typeof googleAd_LB3 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_LB3]);								
			if(typeof googleAd_LB4 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_LB4]);
			if(typeof googleAd_LB5 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_LB5]);								
			if(typeof googleAd_WS1 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_WS1]);
			if(typeof googleAd_WS2 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_WS2]);
			if(typeof googleAd_BB1 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_BB1]);
			if(typeof googleAd_BB2 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_BB2]);
			if(typeof googleAd_BB3 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_BB3]);								
			if(typeof googleAd_PX1 != "undefined") googletag.pubads().refresh([googleAd_PX1]);								
		}

   if (!("ontouchstart" in document.documentElement)) {
			$$(".icon-box").addClass("hover-icon-box");

		var noti_num = $$('#notification-num');
		var popupNotification = $$('#popup-notification');
		showNotiNum(noti_num);

		$$("#popup-quicklink .edit-btn").click(function() {
			$$(this).text(function(i, text){
				return text === "編輯" ? "完成" : "編輯";
			});
			if ($$(this).text() === "編輯") {
				var removeFid = [];
				$$("#popup-quicklink .mark-delete").each(function() {
					removeFid.push($$(this).data('fid-row'));
				});
				if (removeFid) {
					$$.getJSON('json_quicklink.php?action=removeQuickLink&removeFid=' + removeFid.join(','), function(data) {
						if (data['status']['type'] === 'success') {
							$$("#popup-quicklink .mark-delete").fadeOut("normal", function() {
								$$(this).remove();
							});
						} else {
							alert('系統錯誤，請稍後再嘗試');
						}
					});
				}
			}
			$$("#popup-quicklink .delete-btn").toggle();
		});
		$$("#popup-quicklink .delete-btn").click(function() {
			if ($$(this).parent().hasClass('mark-delete')) {
				$$(this).parent().removeClass('mark-delete');
			} else {
				$$(this).parent().addClass('mark-delete');
			}
		});
				$$("body").click(function(){
			hideNotiOdj(popupNotification);
		});
  </script>
  <script language="javascript">
   function submithotkeywordsearch(obj){
			searchtype(1, '搜尋');
			document.getElementById("searchform").elements["srchtxt"].value = obj.innerHTML;
			ga_trackEvent(null,'Homepage Hot Keyword',obj.innerHTML);
			document.getElementById("searchform").setAttribute("target", "_blank");
			document.getElementById("searchform").submit();
		}

		function showSearchMenu(){
			document.getElementById("search-box-menu").style.display = "block";
		}

		function hideSearchMenu(){
			document.getElementById("search-box-menu").style.display = "none";
		}

		function changeSearchAction(searchengine){
			document.searchform.srcheng.value = searchengine;
			document.searchform.target = '_self';
			if(searchengine==1){
				document.searchform.action = 'search.php';
			}else if(searchengine==2){ //advance search
				window.location = 'search.php';
			}
		}

		function searchtype(id, txt) {
			document.getElementById('search-box-menu').style.display = 'none';
			document.getElementById('current-search-item').innerHTML = txt;
			changeSearchAction(id);
		}

		function checkSrchtxt(txt){
			var srcheng = document.searchform.srcheng.value;
			if(srcheng!=2 && trim(txt.value)==''){
				alert('請輸入搜尋字詞');
				txt.focus();
				return false;
			}
			changeSearchAction(srcheng);
			return true;
		}
  </script>

     <!-- Hotlive V2 Script -->
     <script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
      var live_timer_in;
        var live_timer_out;
        var hotlive_page = 0;
        is_hotlive_array = {};

        //	auto change page while mouseenter #hot-live-main-box
        var autoChange = null;
        var timeInterval = 14000;
        var mouseState = false;
        var disableScroll = false;
        var loading = false;

        $$(function (e) {
        	
            $$('body').on('mouseenter', '#hot-live-main-box', function () {
                mouseState = true
                HotLiveBoxShow();
                if (!disableScroll) {
                    autoChange = setInterval(nextPage, timeInterval);
                }
            })

            $$('body').on('mouseleave', '#hot-live-main-box', function () {
                mouseState = false
                clearInterval(autoChange);
                HotLiveBoxHide();
            })

            $$('body').on('click', '#hot-live-scroll-left', function () {
                disableScroll = true;
                if (hotlive_page > 0) {
                    hotlive_page -= 1;
                    switchPage(hotlive_page)
                }
            });

            $$('body').on('click', '#hot-live-scroll-right',function () {
                disableScroll = true;
                nextPage();
            });


            $$('body').on({
                mouseenter: function(){
                    hover()
                },
                mouseleave: function(){
                    hoverLeave()
                }
            }, '#hot-live-scroll-left, #hot-live-scroll-right');

			        });

        function hover() {
            clearInterval(autoChange);
        }

        function hoverLeave() {
            clearInterval(autoChange);
            if (mouseState && !disableScroll)
                autoChange = setInterval(nextPage, timeInterval);
        }

        function switchPage(hotlive_page) {
            $$('#hot-live-box').animate({scrollLeft: 898 * hotlive_page}, 200);
            hotlive_trackEvent(hotlive_page);
            show_hotlive_paging_btn(hotlive_page);
        }

        function nextPage() {
            if (hotlive_page < getShowPage() - 1) {
                hotlive_page += 1;
                switchPage(hotlive_page)
            } else if (hotlive_page === getShowPage() - 1) {
                hotlive_page = 0;
                switchPage(hotlive_page)
            }
        }

        function show_hotlive_paging_btn(func_page) {
            if (getShowPage() <= 1) {
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'none');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'none');
                return
            }
            if (func_page == 0) {
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'none');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'block');
            } else if (func_page == getShowPage() - 1) {

                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'block');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'none');
            } else {
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'block');
                $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'block');
            }
        }

        function hotlive_trackEvent(page) {
            if (is_hotlive_array[page]) {
                return;
            }
            if (typeof dataLayer != "undefined") {
                dataLayer.push({
                    'event': 'HotliveEvent',
                    'eventPage': (page + 2)
                });
            }
            is_hotlive_array[page] = true;
        }

        function HotLiveBoxHide() {
            if (live_timer_in) {
                clearTimeout(live_timer_in);
            }
            live_timer_out = setTimeout(function () {
                HotLiveBoxHideFunction();
            }, 300)
        }

        function HotLiveBoxShow() {
            if (live_timer_out) {
                clearTimeout(live_timer_out);
            }

            live_timer_in = setTimeout(function () {
                HotLiveBoxShowFunction();
            }, 300)
        }

        function HotLiveBoxHideFunction() {
            //clearTimeout(live_timer);
            $$('#hot-live-box').stop();
            //$$('#hot-live-box').animate({width:'242px'}, 500);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box').animate({width: '242px'}, 300);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').stop();
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').css('display', 'block');
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').animate({opacity: 100}, 300);


            $$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display', 'none');
            $$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display', 'none');
        }

        function HotLiveBoxShowFunction() {
            $$('#hot-live-box').stop();
            $$('#hot-live-box').animate({width: '898px'}, 100);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box').animate({width: '898px'}, 300);
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').stop();
            $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').animate({opacity: 0}, 300, function () {
                $$('#hot-live-main-box .live-box-more-bar').css('display', 'none');
                ga_trackEvent('', 'Homepage Live Topics', 'open');
                hotlive_trackEvent(hotlive_page);
                // add fire counter for abtest21 hotlive expand event
                window.firehlexpanded = true;
            });

            show_hotlive_paging_btn(hotlive_page);
            //$$('#hot-live-scroll-left').css('display','block');
            //$$('#hot-live-scroll-right').css('display','block');
        }

        function getShowPage() {
            const page = $$("input[name='showPageTmp']").val()
            if (!!page) {
                return parseInt(page)
            }
            return 20        }

        function hotliveLoaded() {
            abtest21_trackingVar = JSON.parse($$("input[name='trackingVarTmp']").val())
            if (typeof dataLayer != "undefined") {
                dataLayer.push({
                    'event': 'HotliveSwitchTabEvent',
                    'eventPage': (1)
                });
            }
            HotLiveBoxShow()
            hotlive_page = 0;
            is_hotlive_array = {};
            autoChange = null;
            mouseState = true;
            disableScroll = false;
            loading = false;
            autoChange = setInterval(nextPage, timeInterval);
        }
     </script>

       // quick link button
            $$(function () {
                var timer;
                $$("#scTab").on('click', function () {
                    if ($$("#sc").is(':hidden')) {
                        setcookie('cdb_quicklink_state', 1, 86400, '/', 'discuss.com.hk');  // it will open, change state to 1
                    } else {
                        setcookie('cdb_quicklink_state', 0, 86400, '/', 'discuss.com.hk');
                    }
                    $$("#sc").slideToggle();
                });
                $$("#qmark_icon").hover(function () {
                    clearTimeout(timer);
                    timer = setTimeout(function () {
                        $$("#qmark_content").show(0);
                    }, 500)
                }, function () {
                    clearTimeout(timer);
                    $$("#qmark_content").hide(0);
                })
            })
      </script>
